His saying: {ijtabahu (He chose him)} means: He selected him and singled him out, as He said: {And We had certainly given Ibrahim his sound judgment before, and We were of him well Knowing} [al-Anbiya: 51].

Then He said: {and guided him to a straight path}, which is the worship of Allah alone, without partner, according to a pleasing legislated way.

His saying: {and We gave him good in this world} means: We gathered for him the good of this world from all that a believer needs for the completion of his good life, {and indeed, in the Hereafter he is among the righteous}.

Mujahid said regarding His saying: {and We gave him good in this world}: it means a truthful tongue (a good mention among later generations).

His saying: {Then We revealed to you, [O Muhammad], to follow the religion of Ibrahim, a hanif} means: and among his perfection, his greatness, and the soundness of his tawhid and his path, is that We revealed to you, O Seal of the Messengers and Master of the Prophets: {to follow the religion of Ibrahim, a hanif, and he was not of the polytheists}, as He said in Surah al-An'am: {Say, "Indeed, my Lord has guided me to a straight path, a correct religion, the religion of Ibrahim, a hanif, and he was not of the polytheists"} [al-An'am: 161]. Then Allah Ta'ala said, denouncing the Jews.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَمْدَحُ [تَبَارَكَ وَ] تَعَالَى عَبْدَهُ وَرَسُولَهُ وَخَلِيلَهُ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، إِمَامَ الْحُنَفَاءِ وَوَالِدَ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ، وَيُبَرِّئُهُ مِنَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ، وَمِنَ الْيَهُودِيَّةِ وَالنَّصْرَانِيَّةِ فَقَالَ: ﴿إِنَّ إِبْرَاهِيمَ كَانَ أُمَّةً قَانِتًا لِلَّهِ حَنِيفًا﴾ فَأَمَّا "الْأُمَّةُ"، فهو الْإِمَامُ الَّذِي يُقْتَدَى بِهِ. وَالْقَانِتُ: هُوَ الْخَاشِعُ الْمُطِيعُ. وَالْحَنِيفُ: الْمُنْحَرِفُ قَصْدًا عَنِ الشِّرْكِ إِلَى التَّوْحِيدِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَلَمْ يَكُ مِنَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ﴾

قَالَ سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنْ سَلَمَةَ بْنِ كُهَيْل، عَنْ مُسْلِمٍ البَطِين، عَنْ أَبِي الْعُبَيْدَيْنِ: أَنَّهُ سَأَلَ عَبْدَ اللَّهِ بْنَ مَسْعُودٍ عَنِ الْأُمَّةِ الْقَانِتِ، فَقَالَ: الْأُمَّةُ: مُعَلِّمُ الْخَيْرِ، وَالْقَانِتُ: الْمُطِيعُ لِلَّهِ وَرَسُولِهِ.

وَعَنْ مَالِكٍ قَالَ: قَالَ ابْنُ عُمَرَ: الْأُمَّةُ الَّذِي يُعَلِّمُ النَّاسَ دِينَهُمْ.

وَقَالَ الْأَعْمَشُ، [عَنِ الْحَكَمِ] عَنْ يَحْيَى بْنِ الْجَزَّارِ، عَنْ أَبِي العُبَيدين؛ أَنَّهُ جَاءَ إِلَى عَبْدِ اللَّهِ فَقَالَ: مَنْ نَسْأَلُ إِذَا لَمْ نَسْأَلْكَ؟ فَكَأَنَّ ابْنَ مَسْعُودٍ رقَّ لَهُ، فَقَالَ: أَخْبِرْنِي عَنِ الْأُمَّةِ فَقَالَ: الَّذِي يُعَلِّمُ النَّاسَ الْخَيْرَ.

وَقَالَ الشَّعْبِيُّ: حَدَّثَنِي فروَة بْنُ نَوْفَلٍ الْأَشْجَعِيُّ قَالَ: قَالَ ابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ: إِنَّ مُعَاذًا كَانَ أُمَّةً قَانِتًا لِلَّهِ حَنِيفًا، فَقُلْتُ فِي نَفْسِي: غَلِطَ أَبُو عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، إِنَّمَا قَالَ اللَّهُ: ﴿إِنَّ إِبْرَاهِيمَ كَانَ أُمَّةً﴾ فَقَالَ: أَتَدْرِي مَا الْأُمَّةُ وَمَا الْقَانِتُ؟ قُلْتُ: اللَّهُ [وَرَسُولُهُ] أَعْلَمُ. قَالَ: الْأُمَّةُ الَّذِي يُعَلِّمُ [النَّاسَ] الْخَيْرَ. وَالْقَانِتُ: الْمُطِيعُ لِلَّهِ وَرَسُولِهِ. وَكَذَلِكَ كَانَ مَعَاذٌ مُعَلِّمَ الْخَيْرِ. وَكَانَ مُطِيعًا لِلَّهِ وَرَسُولِهِ.

وَقَدْ رُوِيَ مِنْ غَيْرِ وَجْهٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ؛ حَرَّرَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ .

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: ﴿أُمَّةً﴾ أَيْ: أُمَّةً وَحْدَهُ، وَالْقَانِتُ: الْمُطِيعُ. وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ أَيْضًا: كَانَ إِبْرَاهِيمُ أُمَّةً، أَيْ: مُؤْمِنًا وَحْدَهُ، وَالنَّاسُ كُلُّهُمْ إِذْ ذَاكَ كُفَّارٌ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: كَانَ إِمَامَ هُدى، وَالْقَانِتُ: الْمُطِيعُ لِلَّهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿شَاكِرًا لأنْعُمِهِ﴾ أَيْ: قَائِمًا بِشُكْرِ نِعَمِ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهِ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَإِبْرَاهِيمَ الَّذِي وَفَّى﴾ [النَّجْمِ: ٣٧] ، أَيْ: قَامَ بِجَمِيعِ مَا أَمَرَهُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى بِهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿اجْتَبَاهُ﴾ أَيِ: اخْتَارَهُ وَاصْطَفَاهُ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَلَقَدْ آتَيْنَا إِبْرَاهِيمَ رُشْدَهُ مِنْ قَبْلُ وَكُنَّا بِهِ عَالِمِينَ﴾ [الْأَنْبِيَاءِ: ٥١] .

ثُمَّ قَالَ: ﴿وَهَدَاهُ إِلَى صِرَاطٍ مُسْتَقِيمٍ﴾ وَهُوَ عِبَادَةُ اللَّهِ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ عَلَى شَرْعٍ مَرْضِيٍّ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَآتَيْنَاهُ فِي الدُّنْيَا حَسَنَةً﴾ أَيْ: جَمَعْنَا لَهُ خَيْرَ الدُّنْيَا مِنْ جَمِيعِ مَا يَحْتَاجُ الْمُؤْمِنُ إِلَيْهِ فِي إِكْمَالِ حَيَاتِهِ الطَّيِّبَةِ، ﴿وَإِنَّهُ فِي الآخِرَةِ لَمِنَ الصَّالِحِينَ﴾

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَآتَيْنَاهُ فِي الدُّنْيَا حَسَنَةً﴾ أي: لسان صدق.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿ثُمَّ أَوْحَيْنَا إِلَيْكَ أَنِ اتَّبِعْ مِلَّةَ إِبْرَاهِيمَ حَنِيفًا﴾ أَيْ: وَمِنْ كَمَالِهِ وَعَظَمَتِهِ وَصِحَّةِ تَوْحِيدِهِ وَطَرِيقِهِ، أَنَّا أَوْحَيْنَا إِلَيْكَ يَا خَاتَمَ الرُّسُلِ وَسَيِّدَ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ: ﴿أَنِ اتَّبِعْ مِلَّةَ إِبْرَاهِيمَ حَنِيفًا وَمَا كَانَ مِنَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ﴾ كَمَا قَالَ: فِي "الْأَنْعَامِ": ﴿قُلْ إِنَّنِي هَدَانِي رَبِّي إِلَى صِرَاطٍ مُسْتَقِيمٍ دِينًا قِيَمًا مِلَّةَ إِبْرَاهِيمَ حَنِيفًا وَمَا كَانَ مِنَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ١٦١] ، ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى مُنْكِرًا عَلَى الْيَهُودِ.

---

## 16:124 — verse 124

### Translation

There is no doubt that God, Exalted is He, prescribed for every religious community a day of the week on which people would gather for worship. He prescribed for this nation the day of Jumu'ah (Friday), because it is the sixth day on which God completed the creation, on which [people] gathered, and on which the blessing upon His servants was perfected. It is also said that He, Exalted is He, prescribed this for the Children of Israel through the tongue of Moses (peace be upon him), but they turned away from it and chose the Sabbath instead, because it was the day on which the Lord did not create any of the creatures whose creation He had completed on Friday. So He bound them to it in the law of the Torah, and enjoined them to hold fast to it and to observe it, along with commanding them to follow Muhammad ﷺ when he would be sent. He took their covenants and pledges upon that. This is why He, Exalted is He, said: {The Sabbath was only made obligatory for those who differed concerning it}.

Mujahid said: they followed it and abandoned Jumu'ah.

Then they continued to hold fast to it until God sent Jesus son of Mary (peace be upon him). It is said that he shifted them to Sunday. It is also said that he did not abandon the law of the Torah except what was abrogated of some of its rulings, and that he continued to observe the Sabbath until he was raised up, and that it was the Christians after him, in the time of Constantine, who shifted to Sunday in opposition to the Jews, and turned toward the east of the Rock in their prayer. And God knows best.

It is established in the two Sahihs, from the hadith of Abd al-Razzaq, from Ma'mar, from Hammam, from Abu Hurayrah, may God be pleased with him, that he heard the Messenger of God ﷺ say: "We are the last, the foremost on the Day of Resurrection, except that they were given the Book before us. Then this is their day which God made obligatory upon them, but they differed concerning it, so God guided us to it. So the people follow us in regard to it: the Jews tomorrow, and the Christians the day after tomorrow." This is the wording of al-Bukhari.

And from Abu Hurayrah and Hudhayfah, may God be pleased with them both, they said: the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "God led astray from Jumu'ah those who came before us. So the Jews had Saturday, and the Christians had Sunday. Then God brought us and guided us to the day of Jumu'ah. So He established Friday, Saturday, and Sunday, and thus they follow us on the Day of Resurrection. We are the last of the people of this world and the first on the Day of Resurrection, and the judgment concerning them will be rendered before all other creatures." Narrated by Muslim. [And God knows best.]

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

لَا شَكَّ أَنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى شرَع فِي كُلِّ مِلَّةٍ يَوْمًا مِنَ الْأُسْبُوعِ، يَجْتَمِعُ النَّاسُ فِيهِ لِلْعِبَادَةِ، فَشَرَعَ تَعَالَى لِهَذِهِ الْأُمَّةِ يَوْمَ الْجُمْعَةِ؛ لِأَنَّهُ الْيَوْمُ السَّادِسُ الَّذِي أَكْمَلَ اللَّهُ فِيهِ الْخَلِيقَةَ، وَاجْتَمَعَتِ [النَّاسُ] فِيهِ وَتَمَّتِ النِّعْمَةُ عَلَى عِبَادِهِ. وَيُقَالُ: إِنَّهُ تَعَالَى شَرَعَ ذَلِكَ لِبَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ عَلَى لِسَانِ مُوسَى، فَعَدَلُوا عَنْهُ وَاخْتَارُوا السَّبْتَ؛ لِأَنَّهُ الْيَوْمُ الَّذِي لَمْ يَخْلُقْ فِيهِ الرَّبُّ شَيْئًا مِنَ الْمَخْلُوقَاتِ الَّذِي كَمَّلَ خَلْقَهَا يَوْمَ الْجُمْعَةِ، فَأَلْزَمَهُمْ تَعَالَى بِهِ فِي شَرِيعَةِ التَّوْرَاةِ، وَوَصَّاهُمْ أَنْ يَتَمَسَّكُوا بِهِ وَأَنْ يُحَافِظُوا عَلَيْهِ، مَعَ أَمْرِهِ إِيَّاهُمْ بِمُتَابَعَةِ مُحَمَّدٍ صلى الله عليه وسلم إذا بعثه. وأخذه مَوَاثِيقَهُمْ وَعُهُودَهُمْ عَلَى ذَلِكَ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّمَا جُعِلَ السَّبْتُ عَلَى الَّذِينَ اخْتَلَفُوا فِيهِ﴾

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: اتَّبَعُوهُ وَتَرَكُوا الْجُمْعَةَ.

ثُمَّ إِنَّهُمْ لَمْ يَزَالُوا مُتَمَسِّكِينَ بِهِ، حَتَّى بَعَثَ اللَّهُ عِيسَى ابْنَ مَرْيَمَ، فَيُقَالُ: إِنَّهُ حوَّلهم إِلَى يَوْمِ الْأَحَدِ. وَيُقَالُ إِنَّهُ: لَمْ [يَتْرُكْ شَرِيعَةَ التَّوْرَاةِ إِلَّا مَا نُسِخَ مِنْ بَعْضِ أَحْكَامِهَا وَإِنَّهُ لِمْ] يَزَلْ مُحَافِظًا عَلَى السَّبْتِ حَتَّى رُفِعَ، وَإِنَّ النَّصَارَى بَعْدَهُ فِي زَمَنِ قُسْطَنْطِينَ هُمُ الَّذِينَ تَحَوَّلُوا إِلَى يَوْمِ الْأَحَدِ، مُخَالَفَةً لِلْيَهُودِ، وَتَحَوَّلُوا إِلَى الصَّلَاةِ شَرْقًا عَنِ الصَّخْرَةِ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَدْ ثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ، عَنْ مَعْمَر، عَنْ هَمَّامٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم يَقُولُ: "نَحْنُ الْآخِرُونَ السَّابِقُونَ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، بِيْدَ أَنَّهُمْ أُوتُوا الْكِتَابَ مِنْ قَبْلِنَا، ثُمَّ هَذَا يَوْمُهُمُ الَّذِي فَرَضَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمْ فَاخْتَلَفُوا فِيهِ، فَهَدَانَا اللَّهُ لَهُ، فَالنَّاسُ لَنَا فِيهِ تَبَعٌ، الْيَهُودُ غَدًا، وَالنَّصَارَى بَعْدَ غَدٍ". لَفْظُ الْبُخَارِيِّ .

وَعَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، وَحُذَيْفَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا، قَالَا قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أَضَلَّ اللَّهُ عَنِ الْجُمُعَةِ مَنْ كَانَ قَبْلَنَا، فَكَانَ لِلْيَهُودِ يَوْمُ السَّبْتَ، وَكَانَ لِلنَّصَارَى يَوْمُ الْأَحَدِ، فَجَاءَ اللَّهُ بِنَا فَهَدَانَا اللَّهُ ليوم الْجُمُعَةِ، فَجَعَلَ الْجُمُعَةَ وَالسَّبْتَ وَالْأَحَدَ، وَكَذَلِكَ هُمْ تَبَعٌ لَنَا يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، نَحْنُ الْآخِرُونَ مِنْ أَهْلِ الدُّنْيَا وَالْأَوَّلُونَ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، وَالْمَقْضِيُّ بَيْنَهُمْ قَبْلَ الْخَلَائِقِ". رَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ [وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ] .

---

## 16:125 — verse 125

### Translation

The Exalted says, commanding His Messenger Muhammad ﷺ to call creation to Allah {with wisdom}.

Ibn Jarir said: this is what He sent down to him of the Book and the Sunnah. {And goodly exhortation}, that is, by means of what it contains of warnings and accounts of what befell peoples, by which he reminds them, so that they may beware of the punishment of Allah the Exalted.

His saying, {and argue with them in the manner that is best}, means: whoever among them needs to be debated and argued with, let it be done in a good manner, with gentleness, softness, and fine speech, just as He said: {And do not argue with the People of the Book except in the manner that is best, except for those among them who commit wrong} [al-Ankabut: 46]. So He commanded him to be gentle in approach, just as He commanded Musa and Harun (peace be upon them) when He sent them to Pharaoh, saying: {So speak to him gentle speech, that perhaps he may remember or fear} [Ta-Ha: 44].

His saying, {Indeed your Lord is most knowing of who has strayed from His way, and He is most knowing of the rightly guided}, means: He had already known beforehand who among them was doomed and who was blessed, and He recorded that with Him and had finished with the matter. So call them to Allah, and do not let your soul be consumed with grief over those among them who have strayed, for their guidance is not your responsibility. You are only a warner; upon you is the conveyance of the message, and upon Us is the reckoning. {Indeed you do not guide whom you love} [al-Qasas: 56], and {their guidance is not your responsibility} [al-Baqarah: 272].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى آمِرًا رَسُولَهُ مُحَمَّدًا ﷺ أَنْ يَدْعُوَ الْخَلْقَ إِلَى اللَّهِ ﴿بِالْحِكْمَةِ﴾

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: وَهُوَ مَا أَنْزَلَهُ عَلَيْهِ مِنَ الْكِتَابِ وَالسُّنَّةِ ﴿وَالْمَوْعِظَةِ الْحَسَنَةِ﴾ أَيْ: بِمَا فِيهِ مِنَ الزَّوَاجِرِ وَالْوَقَائِعِ بِالنَّاسِ ذَكَّرَهُمْ بِهَا، لِيَحْذَرُوا بَأْسَ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَجَادِلْهُمْ بِالَّتِي هِيَ أَحْسَنُ﴾ أَيْ: مَنِ احْتَاجَ مِنْهُمْ إِلَى مُنَاظَرَةٍ وَجِدَالٍ، فَلْيَكُنْ بِالْوَجْهِ الْحَسَنِ بِرِفْقٍ وَلِينٍ وَحُسْنِ خِطَابٍ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَلا تُجَادِلُوا أَهْلَ الْكِتَابِ إِلا بِالَّتِي هِيَ أَحْسَنُ إِلا الَّذِينَ ظَلَمُوا مِنْهُمْ﴾ [الْعَنْكَبُوتِ: ٤٦] فَأَمَرَهُ تَعَالَى بِلِينِ الْجَانِبِ، كَمَا أَمَرَ مُوسَى وَهَارُونَ، عَلَيْهِمَا السَّلَامُ، حِينَ بَعَثَهُمَا إِلَى فِرْعَوْنَ فَقَالَ: ﴿فَقُولا لَهُ قَوْلا لَيِّنًا لَعَلَّهُ يَتَذَكَّرُ أَوْ يَخْشَى﴾ [طه: ٤٤] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنَّ رَبَّكَ هُوَ أَعْلَمُ بِمَنْ ضَلَّ عَنْ سَبِيلِهِ وَهُوَ أَعْلَمُ بِالْمُهْتَدِينَ﴾ أي: قدم عَلِمَ الشَّقِيَّ مِنْهُمْ وَالسَّعِيدَ، وَكَتَبَ ذَلِكَ عِنْدَهُ وَفَرَغَ مِنْهُ، فَادْعُهُمْ إِلَى اللَّهِ، وَلَا تَذْهَبْ نَفْسُكَ عَلَى مَنْ ضَلَّ مِنْهُمْ حَسَرَاتٍ، فَإِنَّهُ لَيْسَ عَلَيْكَ هُدَاهُمْ إِنَّمَا أَنْتَ نَذِيرٌ، عَلَيْكَ الْبَلَاغُ، وَعَلَيْنَا الْحِسَابُ، ﴿إِنَّكَ لَا تَهْدِي مَنْ أَحْبَبْتَ﴾ [الْقَصَصِ: ٥٦] ، وَ ﴿لَيْسَ عَلَيْكَ هُدَاهُمْ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ٢٧٢] .

---

## 16:126-128 — verses 126-128 (shared commentary)

### Translation

He, the Exalted, commands justice in retaliation and equivalence in obtaining one's right, as Abd al-Razzaq said, from al-Thawri, from Khalid, from Ibn Sirin, that he said concerning His statement, the Exalted: {Then retaliate in the manner in which you were made to suffer}: "If a man takes something from you, take from him the equivalent of it."

Mujahid, Ibrahim, al-Hasan al-Basri and others said likewise, and Ibn Jarir preferred this view.

Ibn Zayd said: They had been commanded to overlook the polytheists, then some men of standing embraced Islam and said, "O Messenger of God, if God permitted us we would take revenge upon these dogs!" So this verse was revealed, then that ruling was abrogated by the command to wage jihad.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said, from one of his companions, from Ata ibn Yasar, who said: The entire surah of al-Nahl was revealed in Makkah, and it is Makkan except for the last three verses, which were revealed in Madinah after Uhud, when Hamzah, may God be pleased with him, was killed and mutilated. The Messenger of God ﷺ said, "If we prevail over them, we will surely mutilate thirty men of theirs." When the Muslims heard that, they said, "By God, if we prevail over them we will mutilate them with a mutilation the like of which no Arab has ever inflicted upon anyone." So God revealed: {And if you punish, then punish with the equivalent of that with which you were harmed} to the end of the surah.

This is mursal (a report missing the Companion link), and it contains an unnamed man who is not identified. This has also been narrated through another connected chain. Al-Hafiz Abu Bakr al-Bazzar said:

[chain] al-Hasan ibn Yahya, Amr ibn Asim, Salih al-Murri, from Sulayman al-Taymi, from Abu Uthman, from Abu Hurayrah, may God be pleased with him: that the Messenger of God ﷺ stood over Hamzah ibn Abd al-Muttalib, may God be pleased with him, when he was martyred, and looked upon a sight more painful to the heart than any he had ever seen, or he said "to his heart than it." He looked at him, having been mutilated, and said: "May God's mercy be upon you. Indeed you were, as far as I knew, one who maintained the ties of kinship and did much good. By God, were it not for the grief of those who will come after you over you, it would have pleased me to leave you until God gathers you from the bellies of beasts of prey," or words to that effect, "but by God, over this I will surely mutilate seventy of them as they mutilated you." Then Gabriel (peace be upon him) descended upon Muhammad ﷺ with this surah and recited: {And if you punish, then punish with the equivalent of that with which you were harmed} to the end of the verse. So the Messenger of God ﷺ made expiation, that is, for his oath, and refrained from that.

This chain contains weakness, because Salih, who is Ibn Bashir al-Murri, is weak according to the scholars of hadith, and al-Bukhari said: "He is one whose hadith is rejected (munkar al-hadith)."

Al-Sha'bi and Ibn Jurayj said: It was revealed concerning the statement of the Muslims on the day of Uhud regarding those who had been mutilated: "We will surely mutilate them." So God revealed this concerning them.

Abd Allah ibn al-Imam Ahmad said in the Musnad of his father: [chain] Hudayyah ibn Abd al-Wahhab al-Marwazi, al-Fadl ibn Musa, Isa ibn Ubayd, from al-Rabi ibn Anas, from Abu al-Aliyah, from Ubayy ibn Ka'b, who said: On the day of Uhud, sixty men of the Ansar were killed and six of the Muhajirun. The Companions of the Messenger of God ﷺ said, "If we ever have a day like this against the polytheists, we will surely exceed them in retaliation." Then on the day of the Conquest, a man said, "Quraysh will no longer be recognized after today." So a caller announced: "The Messenger of God ﷺ has granted safety to black and white alike, except so-and-so and so-and-so," naming certain people. Then God, blessed and exalted, revealed: {And if you punish, then punish with the equivalent of that with which you were harmed, but if you are patient, it is certainly better for the patient}. The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "We will be patient and not punish."

This noble verse has parallels in the Qur'an, for it comprises the legislation of justice and encouragement toward what is more excellent, as in His statement: {The recompense for an evil is an evil equivalent to it}, then He said {but whoever pardons and reconciles, his reward is upon God} [al-Shura: 40]. And He said {and wounds are subject to retaliation in kind}, then He said {but whoever forgoes it as charity, it is an expiation for him} [al-Ma'idah: 45]. And He said in this noble verse: {And if you punish, then punish with the equivalent of that with which you were harmed}, then He said {but if you are patient, it is certainly better for the patient}.

His statement: {And be patient, and your patience is not but through God} is an emphasis of the command to patience, and an informing that this is attained only through God's will, His aid, His power and His strength.

Then He, the Exalted, said: {And do not grieve over them}, meaning: over those who opposed you, do not grieve over them, for God has decreed that. {And do not be in distress}, meaning: in anguish, {over what they plot}, meaning: over the effort they exert against themselves in their enmity toward you and in bringing harm to you, for God suffices you, supports you, aids you, grants you victory, and gives you triumph over them.

His statement: {Indeed, God is with those who fear Him and those who are doers of good} means: with them through His support, His aid and His assistance. This is a special divine companionship (ma'iyyah khassah), as in His statement: {When your Lord revealed to the angels, "I am with you, so make firm those who believe"} [al-Anfal: 12], and His statement to Musa and Harun (peace be upon them): {Do not fear, indeed I am with you both, I hear and I see} [Ta Ha: 46], and the statement of the Prophet ﷺ to al-Siddiq while the two of them were in the cave: {Do not grieve, indeed God is with us} [al-Tawbah: 40]. As for the general divine companionship (ma'iyyah ammah), it is through hearing, sight and knowledge, as in His statement, the Exalted: {And He is with you wherever you are, and God is All-Seeing of what you do} [al-Hadid: 4], and as in His statement, the Exalted: {Do you not see that God knows what is in the heavens and what is on the earth? There is no secret consultation among three but that He is their fourth, nor among five but that He is their sixth, nor less than that nor more but that He is with them wherever they are} [al-Mujadalah: 7], and as He, the Exalted, said: {You are not engaged in any matter, nor do you recite any portion of the Qur'an, nor do you do any deed, but that We are witnesses over you when you are engaged in it. Nothing escapes your Lord, even the weight of an atom, on the earth or in the heaven, nor anything smaller than that or greater, but it is in a clear register} [Yunus: 61].

The meaning of {those who fear Him} is: those who abandon what is forbidden, and {those who are doers of good} means: those who perform acts of obedience. These are the ones whom God preserves and guards, whom He supports and aids, and to whom He grants victory over their enemies and opponents.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] my father, Muhammad ibn Bashshar, Abu Ahmad al-Zubayri, Mis'ar, from Ibn Awn, from Muhammad ibn Hatib, who said: Uthman, may God be pleased with him, was among those who believed, among those who feared God, and among those who were doers of good.

[End of the tafsir of Surat al-Nahl. All praise belongs to God entirely, and all favor. In Him is the aid sought, and He suffices us, and He is the best Guardian.]

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَأْمُرُ تَعَالَى بِالْعَدْلِ فِي الِاقْتِصَاصِ وَالْمُمَاثَلَةِ فِي اسْتِيفَاءِ الْحَقِّ، كَمَا قَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ، عَنِ الثَّوْرِيِّ، عَنْ خَالِدٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ سِيرِينَ: أَنَّهُ قَالَ فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَعَاقِبُوا بِمِثْلِ مَا عُوقِبْتُمْ بِهِ﴾ إِنْ أَخَذَ مِنْكُمْ رَجُلٌ شَيْئًا، فَخُذُوا مِنْهُ مِثْلَهُ.

وَكَذَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَإِبْرَاهِيمُ، وَالْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ، وَغَيْرُهُمْ. وَاخْتَارَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ زَيْدٍ: كَانُوا قَدْ أُمِرُوا بِالصَّفْحِ عَنِ الْمُشْرِكِينَ، فَأَسْلَمَ رِجَالٌ ذَوُو منعةٍ، فَقَالُوا: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، لَوْ أَذِنَ اللَّهُ لَنَا لَانْتَصَرْنَا مِنْ هَؤُلَاءِ الْكِلَابِ! فَنَزَلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ، ثُمَّ نُسِخَ ذَلِكَ بِالْجِهَادِ.

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ بَعْضِ أَصْحَابِهِ، عَنْ عَطَاءِ بْنِ يَسَار قَالَ: نَزَلَتْ سُورَةُ "النَّحْلِ" كُلُّهَا بِمَكَّةَ، وَهِيَ مَكِّيَّةٌ إِلَّا ثَلَاثَ آيَاتٍ مِنْ آخِرِهَا نَزَلَتْ بِالْمَدِينَةِ بَعْدَ أُحُدٍ، حَيْثُ قُتِلَ حَمْزَةُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، وَمُثِّلَ بِهِ فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَئِنْ ظَهَرْنَا عَلَيْهِمْ لَنُمَثِّلَنَّ بِثَلَاثِينَ رَجُلًا مِنْهُمْ" فَلَمَّا سَمِعَ الْمُسْلِمُونَ ذَلِكَ قَالُوا: وَاللَّهِ لَئِنْ ظَهَرْنَا عَلَيْهِمْ لَنُمَثِّلَنَّ بِهِمْ مُثْلَةً لَمْ يُمَثِّلْهَا أَحَدٌ مِنَ الْعَرَبِ بِأَحَدٍ قَطُّ. فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ: ﴿وَإِنْ عَاقَبْتُمْ فَعَاقِبُوا بِمِثْلِ مَا عُوقِبْتُمْ بِهِ﴾ إِلَى آخَرِ السُّورَةِ .

وَهَذَا مُرْسَلٌ، وَفِيهِ [رَجُلٌ] مُبْهَمٌ لَمْ يُسَمَّ، وَقَدْ رُوِيَ هَذَا مِنْ وَجْهٍ آخَرَ مُتَّصِلٍ، فَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ الْبَزَّارُ:

حَدَّثَنَا الْحَسَنُ بْنُ يَحْيَى، حَدَّثَنَا عَمْرُو بْنُ عَاصِمٍ، حَدَّثَنَا صَالِحُ الْمُرِّيُّ ، عَنْ سُلَيْمَانَ التَّيْمِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِي عُثْمَانَ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ؛ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَقَفَ عَلَى حَمْزَةَ بْنِ عَبْدِ الْمُطَّلِبِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، حِينَ اسْتُشْهِدَ، فَنَظَرَ إِلَى مَنْظَرٍ لَمْ يَنْظُرْ أَوْجَعَ لِلْقَلْبِ مِنْهُ. أَوْ قَالَ: لِقَلْبِهِ [مِنْهُ] فَنَظَرَ إِلَيْهِ وَقَدْ مُثِّل بِهِ فَقَالَ: "رَحْمَةُ اللَّهِ عَلَيْكَ، إِنْ كُنْتَ -لَمَا علمتُ-لَوَصُولًا لِلرَّحِمِ، فَعُولًا لِلْخَيْرَاتِ، وَاللَّهِ لَوْلَا حُزْنُ مَنْ بَعْدَكَ عَلَيْكَ، لَسَرَّنِي أَنْ أَتْرُكَكَ حَتَّى يَحْشُرَكَ اللَّهُ مِنْ بُطُونِ السِّبَاعِ -أَوْ كَلِمَةً نَحْوَهَا-أَمَا وَاللَّهِ عَلَى ذَلِكَ، لَأُمَثِّلَنَّ بِسَبْعِينَ كَمُثْلَتِكَ . فَنَزَلَ جِبْرِيلُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، عَلَى مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ بِهَذِهِ السُّورَةِ وَقَرَأَ: ﴿وَإِنْ عَاقَبْتُمْ فَعَاقِبُوا بِمِثْلِ مَا عُوقِبْتُمْ بِهِ﴾ إِلَى آخَرِ الْآيَةِ، فَكَفَّرَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ -يَعْنِي: عَنْ يَمِينِهِ-وَأَمْسَكَ عَنْ ذَلِكَ .

وَهَذَا إِسْنَادٌ فِيهِ ضَعْفٌ؛ لِأَنَّ صَالِحًا -هُوَ ابْنُ بَشِيرٍ الْمُرِّيُّ-ضَعِيفٌ عِنْدَ الْأَئِمَّةِ، وَقَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: هُوَ مُنْكَرُ الْحَدِيثِ.

وَقَالَ الشَّعْبِيُّ وَابْنُ جُرَيْج: نَزَلَتْ فِي قَوْلِ الْمُسْلِمِينَ يَوْمَ أُحُدٍ فِيمَنْ مُثِّلَ بِهِمْ: لَنُمَثِّلَنَّ بِهِمْ. فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ فِيهِمْ ذَلِكَ.

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ الْإِمَامِ أَحْمَدَ فِي مُسْنَدِ أَبِيهِ: حَدَّثَنَا هدِيَّة بْنُ عَبْدِ الْوَهَّابِ الْمَرْوَزِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا الْفَضْلُ بْنُ مُوسَى، حَدَّثَنَا عِيسَى بْنُ عُبَيْدٍ، عَنِ الرَّبِيعِ بْنِ أَنَسٍ، عَنْ أَبِي الْعَالِيَةِ، عن أُبَيِّ بْنِ كَعْبٍ قَالَ: لَمَّا كَانَ يَوْمُ أُحُدٍ، قُتِلَ مِنَ الْأَنْصَارِ سِتُّونَ رَجُلًا وَمِنَ الْمُهَاجِرِينَ سِتَّةٌ، فَقَالَ أَصْحَابُ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ: لَئِنْ كَانَ لَنَا يَوْمٌ مِثْلُ هَذَا مِنَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ لَنُرْبِيَنَّ عَلَيْهِمْ. فَلَمَّا كان يوم الفتح قال رجل: لا تُعْرَفُ قُرَيْشٌ بَعْدَ الْيَوْمِ. فَنَادَى مُنَادٍ: إِنْ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ آمَنَ الْأَسْوَدَ وَالْأَبْيَضَ إِلَّا فُلَانًا وَفُلَانًا -نَاسًا سَمَّاهُمْ-فأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ تَبَارَكَ وَتَعَالَى: ﴿وَإِنْ عَاقَبْتُمْ [فَعَاقِبُوا بِمِثْلِ مَا عُوقِبْتُمْ بِهِ وَلَئِنْ صَبَرْتُمْ لَهُوَ خَيْرٌ لِلصَّابِرِينَ] ﴾ فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "نَصْبِرُ وَلَا نُعَاقِبُ" .

وَهَذِهِ الْآيَةُ الْكَرِيمَةُ لَهَا أَمْثَالٌ فِي الْقُرْآنِ، فَإِنَّهَا مُشْتَمِلَةٌ عَلَى مَشْرُوعِيَّةِ الْعَدْلِ وَالنَّدْبِ إِلَى الْفَضْلِ، كَمَا فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَجَزَاءُ سَيِّئَةٍ سَيِّئَةٌ مِثْلُهَا﴾ ثُمَّ قَالَ ﴿فَمَنْ عَفَا وَأَصْلَحَ فَأَجْرُهُ عَلَى اللَّهِ﴾ [الشُّورَى: ٤٠] . وَقَالَ ﴿وَالْجُرُوحَ قِصَاصٌ﴾ ثُمَّ قَالَ ﴿فَمَنْ تَصَدَّقَ بِهِ فَهُوَ كَفَّارَةٌ لَهُ﴾ [الْمَائِدَةِ: ٤٥] ، وَقَالَ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ: ﴿وَإِنْ عَاقَبْتُمْ فَعَاقِبُوا بِمِثْلِ مَا عُوقِبْتُمْ بِهِ﴾ ثُمَّ قَالَ ﴿وَلَئِنْ صَبَرْتُمْ لَهُوَ خَيْرٌ لِلصَّابِرِينَ﴾

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَاصْبِرْ وَمَا صَبْرُكَ إِلا بِاللَّهِ﴾ تَأْكِيدٌ لِلْأَمْرِ بِالصَّبْرِ، وَإِخْبَارٌ بِأَنَّ ذَلِكَ إِنَّمَا يُنَالُ بِمَشِيئَةِ اللَّهِ وَإِعَانَتِهِ، وَحَوْلِهِ وَقُوَّتِهِ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلا تَحْزَنْ عَلَيْهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: عَلَى مَنْ خَالَفَكَ، لَا تَحْزَنْ عَلَيْهِمْ؛ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ قَدَّرَ ذَلِكَ، ﴿وَلا تَكُ فِي ضَيْقٍ﴾ أَيْ: غَمٍّ ﴿مِمَّا يَمْكُرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: مِمَّا يُجْهِدُونَ [أَنْفُسَهُمْ] فِي عَدَاوَتِكَ وَإِيصَالِ الشَّرِّ إِلَيْكَ، فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ كَافِيكَ وَنَاصِرُكَ، وَمُؤَيِّدُكَ، وَمُظْهِرُكَ وَمُظْفِرُكَ بِهِمْ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنَّ اللَّهَ مَعَ الَّذِينَ اتَّقَوْا وَالَّذِينَ هُمْ مُحْسِنُونَ﴾ أَيْ: مَعَهُمْ بِتَأْيِيدِهِ وَنَصْرِهِ وَمَعُونَتِهِ وَهَذِهِ مَعِيَّةٌ خَاصَّةٌ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿إِذْ يُوحِي رَبُّكَ إِلَى الْمَلائِكَةِ أَنِّي مَعَكُمْ فَثَبِّتُوا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا﴾ [الْأَنْفَالِ: ١٢] ، وَقَوْلِهِ لِمُوسَى وَهَارُونَ: ﴿لَا تَخَافَا إِنَّنِي مَعَكُمَا أَسْمَعُ وَأَرَى﴾ [طه: ٤٦] ، وَقَوْلِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ لِلصِّدِّيقِ وَهُمَا فِي الْغَارِ: ﴿لَا تَحْزَنْ إِنَّ اللَّهَ مَعَنَا﴾ [التَّوْبَةِ: ٤٠] وَأَمَّا الْمَعِيَّةُ الْعَامَّةُ فَبِالسَّمْعِ وَالْبَصَرِ وَالْعِلْمِ، كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَهُوَ مَعَكُمْ أَيْنَ مَا كُنْتُمْ وَاللَّهُ بِمَا تَعْمَلُونَ بَصِيرٌ﴾ [الْحَدِيدِ: ٤] ، وَكَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَلَمْ تَرَ أَنَّ اللَّهَ يَعْلَمُ مَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَمَا فِي الأرْضِ مَا يَكُونُ مِنْ نَجْوَى ثَلاثَةٍ إِلا هُوَ رَابِعُهُمْ وَلا خَمْسَةٍ إِلا هُوَ سَادِسُهُمْ وَلا أَدْنَى مِنْ ذَلِكَ وَلا أَكْثَرَ إِلا هُوَ مَعَهُمْ أَيْنَ مَا كَانُوا﴾ [الْمُجَادَلَةِ: ٧] ، وَكَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا تَكُونُ فِي شَأْنٍ وَمَا تَتْلُو مِنْهُ مِنْ قُرْآنٍ وَلا تَعْمَلُونَ مِنْ عَمَلٍ إِلا كُنَّا عَلَيْكُمْ شُهُودًا [إِذْ تُفِيضُونَ فِيهِ وَمَا يَعْزُبُ عَنْ رَبِّكَ مِنْ مِثْقَالِ ذَرَّةٍ فِي الأرْضِ وَلا فِي السَّمَاءِ وَلا أَصْغَرَ مِنْ ذَلِكَ وَلا أَكْبَرَ إِلا فِي كِتَابٍ مُبِينٍ] ﴾ [يُونُسَ: ٦١] . 

وَمَعْنَى: ﴿الَّذِينَ اتَّقَوْا﴾ أَيْ: تَرَكُوا الْمُحَرَّمَاتِ، ﴿وَالَّذِينَ هُمْ مُحْسِنُونَ﴾ أَيْ: فَعَلُوا الطَّاعَاتِ، فَهَؤُلَاءِ اللَّهُ يَحْفَظُهُمْ وَيَكْلَؤُهُمْ، وَيَنْصُرُهُمْ وَيُؤَيِّدُهُمْ، وَيُظْفِرُهُمْ عَلَى أَعْدَائِهِمْ وَمُخَالِفِيهِمْ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ بَشَّارٍ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو أَحْمَدَ الزُّبَيْرِيُّ، حدثنا مِسْعر، عَنِ ابْنِ عَوْنٍ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ حَاطِبٍ قَالَ: كَانَ عُثْمَانُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، مِنَ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا، وَالَّذِينَ اتَّقَوْا، وَالَّذِينَ هُمْ مُحْسِنُونَ.

[آخِرُ تَفْسِيرِ سُورَةِ النَّحْلِ وَلِلَّهِ الْحَمْدُ أَجْمَعُهُ وَالْمِنَّةُ، وَبِهِ الْمُسْتَعَانُ وَهُوَ حَسَبُنَا وَنَعِمَ الوكيل]

---
